  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9.35pt;text-align:left;"><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Pursuant to the requirements of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, the registrant has duly caused this report to be signed on its behalf by the undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</span></p>

 <body style="padding:8px;margin:auto!important;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><img src="img85518887_0.jpg" alt="img85518887_0.jpg" style="width:301px;height:57px;"></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12pt;font-family:'Lato',serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#741b47;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">DIANTHUS THERAPEUTICS HIGHLIGHTS RECENT BUSINESS ACHIEVEMENTS</font><font style="color:#741b47;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#741b47;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">AND REPORTS Q4 AND FY 2024 FINANCIAL RESULTS</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 MaGic trial of DNTH103 in generalized Myasthenia Gravis (gMG) ongoing; top-line results on track for 2H&#x2019;25</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 3 CAPTIVATE trial of DNTH103 in Chronic Inflammatory Demyelinating Polyneuropathy (CIDP) ongoing; interim responder analysis anticipated in 2H&#x2019;26</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 MoMeNtum trial of DNTH103 in Multifocal Motor Neuropathy (MMN) ongoing;</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">top-line results anticipated in 2H&#x2019;26</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">$357.0 million of cash provides runway into 2H&#x2019;27</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">New York City and Waltham, Mass., March 11, 2025</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> &#x2013; Dianthus Therapeutics, Inc. (Nasdaq: DNTH), a clinical-stage biotechnology company dedicated to advancing the next generation of antibody complement therapeutics to treat severe autoimmune diseases, today reported financial results for the fourth quarter and full year ending December 31, 2024 and provided an update on recent business achievements.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;We remain on track to report top-line data in 2H&#x2019;25 from our Phase 2 clinical trial of DNTH103 in gMG, an indication where a best-in-class, potent active C1s and classical pathway inhibitor with the potential for effective and consistent symptom control along with improved safety and convenience could meaningfully advance the standard of care,&#x201d; said Marino Garcia, Chief Executive Officer of Dianthus Therapeutics. &#x201c;We are excited to have initiated our pivotal Phase 3 CAPTIVATE trial in CIDP, which is on track for an interim responder analysis in 2H&#x2019;26, along with top-line results from our Phase 2 trial in MMN.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 Clinical Development</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 is an investigational, clinical-stage, potent monoclonal antibody engineered to selectively target the classical pathway by inhibiting only the active form of the C1s protein, a clinically validated complement target. DNTH103 is enhanced with YTE half-life extension technology designed to enable a more convenient subcutaneous, self-administered injection dosed as infrequently as once every two weeks. DNTH103 has the potential to be a best-in-class pipeline-in-a-product across a range of autoimmune disorders with high unmet need.</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Generalized Myasthenia Gravis (gMG)</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:3.333%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 MaGic gMG trial ongoing:</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> The </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">MaGic tria</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">l</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> is a global, randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled Phase 2 trial in patients with gMG who are acetylcholine receptor (AChR) antibody positive, and it remains on track to report top-line results in 2H&#x2019;25.</font></div></div>
  <p style="margin-left:3.333%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="page-border-spacing"><div style="z-index:-3;flex-direction:column;display:flex;padding-bottom:0.5in;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:3.333%;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:3.333%;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">1</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:3.333%;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">www.dianthustx.com 7 Times Square, Floor 43 New York, NY 10036</font></p></div></div>
  <hr style="margin-inline-start:auto;margin-inline-end:auto;page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Chronic Inflammatory Demyelinating Polyneuropathy (CIDP)</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:3.333%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 3 CAPTIVATE CIDP trial ongoing:</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> The </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">CAPTIVATE trial</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> is a single, global, two-part, randomized withdrawal Phase 3 trial in patients with CIDP, and it remains on track for an interim responder analysis in 2H&#x2019;26. The Company believes this single pivotal trial will support a BLA filing in adult patients with CIDP.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Multifocal Motor Neuropathy (MMN)</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:3.333%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 2 MoMeNtum MMN trial ongoing: </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">The </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">MoMeNtum trial</font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">is a global, randomized, double-blind, placebo-controlled Phase 2 trial in patients with MMN, and it remains on track to report top-line results in 2H&#x2019;26.</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Corporate Updates</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:3.333%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">On March 5, 2025, </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;text-decoration:underline solid;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">John C. King was announced as Chief Commercial Officer and Sujay Kango joined the Company&#x2019;s Board of Directors</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">. Mr. King brings to Dianthus more than 25 years of global commercial leadership experience in biotechnology, including neuromuscular and hematological rare diseases. Mr. Kango is an experienced executive with more than 26 years of experience in the pharmaceutical and biotechnology sector. </font></div></div>

  <p style="margin-left:3.333%;font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div class="item-list-element-wrapper" style="display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:3.333%;word-break:keep-all;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">R&amp;D Expenses</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> - Research and development (R&amp;D) expenses for the year ended December 31, 2024 were $83.1 million, inclusive of $5.6 million of stock-based compensation, compared to $32.8 million for the year ended December 31, 2023, which included $0.9 million of stock-based compensation. This increase in R&amp;D expenses was primarily driven by higher clinical costs, chemistry, manufacturing and controls (CMC) costs and increased headcount to support DNTH103 Phase 2 and Phase 3 development.</font></div></div>

This increase in G&amp;A expenses was primarily due to increased headcount and higher professional services costs.</font></div></div>

  <div class="page-border-spacing"><div style="z-index:-3;flex-direction:column;display:flex;padding-bottom:0.5in;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:3.333%;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:3.333%;text-align:right;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">2</font></p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:9pt;margin-right:3.333%;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#720f3b;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:'Roboto',sans-serif;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">www.dianthustx.com 7 Times Square, Floor 43 New York, NY 10036</font></p></div></div>
  <hr style="margin-inline-start:auto;margin-inline-end:auto;page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;z-index:-3;min-height:0.5in;position:relative;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">About DNTH103</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"><br></font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 is an investigational, clinical-stage, potent monoclonal antibody engineered to selectively target the classical pathway by inhibiting only the active form of the C1s protein, a clinically validated complement target. DNTH103 is enhanced with YTE half-life extension technology designed to enable a more convenient subcutaneous, self-administered injection dosed as infrequently as once every two weeks. Additionally, selective inhibition of the classical complement pathway may lower patient risk of infection from encapsulated bacteria by preserving immune activity of the lectin and alternative pathways. As the classical pathway plays a significant role in disease pathology, DNTH103 has the potential to be a best-in-class pipeline-in-a-product across a range of autoimmune disorders with high unmet need. Dianthus is building a neuromuscular franchise with DNTH103 and anticipates reporting top-line data from the Phase 2 MaGic trial in generalized Myasthenia Gravis in 2H&#x2019;25, the interim responder analysis of the Phase 3 CAPITIVATE trial in Chronic Inflammatory Demyelinating Polyneuropathy in 2H&#x2019;26, and top-line data from the Phase 2 MoMeNtum trial in Multifocal Motor Neuropathy in 2H&#x2019;26.</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">DNTH103 is an investigational agent that is not approved as a therapy in any indication in any jurisdiction worldwide.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">About Dianthus Therapeutics</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;">Dianthus Therapeutics is a clinical-stage biotechnology company dedicated to designing and delivering novel, best-in-class monoclonal antibodies with improved selectivity and potency. Based in New York City and Waltham, Mass., Dianthus is comprised of an experienced team of biotech and pharma executives who are leading the development of next-generation antibody complement therapeutics, aiming to deliver transformative medicines for people living with severe autoimmune and inflammatory diseases.</font><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#666666;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-kerning:none;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
